Packaging Compliance (LUCID / VerpackG) ‚Äî HAIROTICMENVersion 1.0 | Date 2025-10-10OverviewThis guide outlines Germany EPR packaging obligations under VerpackG and registration in the LUCID Packaging Register. Update with your system partner and contract details.Key StepsRegister in LUCID (Zentrale Stelle Verpackungsregister) and obtain registration number.Conclude a dual system contract (e.g., for household packaging) with annual forecasts.Classify packaging material fractions and report volumes periodically (monthly/quarterly/annual).Maintain evidence and invoices; reconcile reported volumes with Packaging_Specifications.xlsx and LUCID_VerpackG_Register.xlsx.Publish registration number in imprint/terms and share with distributors.Controls &amp; EvidenceControl Book ‚Üí C-ESG-002. Refund and Return Policy ‚Äì HAIROTICMEN.deOverviewOur refund and return policy lasts 30 days. If 30 days have passed since your purchase, we can‚Äôt offer you a full refund or exchange.To be eligible for a return, your item must be unused and in the same condition that you received it. It must also be in the original packaging.Several types of goods are exempt from being returned. Perishable goods such as food, flowers, newspapers or magazines cannot be returned. We also do not accept products that are intimate or sanitary goods, hazardous materials, or flammable liquids or gases.Additional Non-returnable Items- Gift cards- Downloadable software products- Some health and personal care itemsTo complete your return, we require a receipt or proof of purchase.Please do not send your purchase back to the manufacturer.Partial RefundsThere are certain situations where only partial refunds are granted:- Book with obvious signs of use- CD, DVD, VHS tape, software, video game, cassette tape, or vinyl record that has been opened- Any item not in its original condition, is damaged or missing parts for reasons not due to our error- Any item that is returned more than 30 days after deliveryRefundsOnce your return is received and inspected, we will send you an email to notify you that we have received your returned item. We will also notify you of the approval or rejection of your refund.If you are approved, then your refund will be processed, and a credit will automatically be applied to your credit card or original method of payment, within a certain number of days.Late or Missing RefundsIf you haven‚Äôt received a refund yet, first check your bank account again.Then contact your credit card company, it may take some time before your refund is officially posted.Next contact your bank. There is often some processing time before a refund is posted.If you‚Äôve done all of this and you still have not received your refund yet, please contact us at {email address}.Sale ItemsOnly regular priced items may be refunded. Sale items cannot be refunded.ExchangesWe only replace items if they are defective or damaged. If you need to exchange it for the same item, send us an email at {email address} and send your item to: {physical address}.GiftsIf the item was marked as a gift when purchased and shipped directly to you, you‚Äôll receive a gift credit for the value of your return. Once the returned item is received, a gift certificate will be mailed to you.If the item wasn‚Äôt marked as a gift when purchased, or the gift giver had the order shipped to themselves to give to you later, we will send a refund to the gift giver and they will find out about your return.Shipping ReturnsTo return your product, you should mail your product to: {physical address}.You will be responsible for paying for your own shipping costs for returning your item. Shipping costs are non-refundable. If you receive a refund, the cost of return shipping will be deducted from your refund.Depending on where you live, the time it may take for your exchanged product to reach you may vary.If you are returning more expensive items, you may consider using a trackable shipping service or purchasing shipping insurance. We don‚Äôt guarantee that we will receive your returned item.Need Help?Contact us at {email address} for questions related to refunds and returns.

Data Flow Logic &amp; MCP Integration ‚Äì HAIROTICMENThis specification defines end-to-end data flows and the Model Context Protocol (MCP) integration for HAIROTICMEN‚Äôs AI-driven stack (OpenAI/Hairo Assistant, Odoo 17 Community on OVH, WooCommerce, Google Drive, n8n, Zapier, Monday.com). It includes tool definitions, transports, auth, schemas, sequencing, error handling, idempotency, security scopes, rate limits, testing, and rollout checklist.1) Design Principles‚Ä¢ Single Source of Truth (SSOT): Odoo is authoritative for financials, inventory, and partner master data. ‚Ä¢ Least-Privilege by Default: AI tools expose only required methods; per-scope keys; short-lived tokens where applicable. ‚Ä¢ Idempotency Everywhere: All write operations accept idempotency_key or use external_id to prevent duplicates. ‚Ä¢ Observability First: Every MCP call returns correlation_id; n8n/Zapier executions are logged and linked to Monday.‚Ä¢ Human-in-the-Loop (HITL): Critical actions (posting invoices, issuing refunds) require explicit confirmation or policy gating.2) MCP Transport &amp; Auth‚Ä¢ Transport: JSON-RPC 2.0 over HTTPS. Server exposes /mcp endpoint with Server-Sent Events (SSE) or HTTP POST. ‚Ä¢ Auth: Bearer tokens (service-scoped) + optional mTLS for server-to-server. ‚Ä¢ Scopes (examples):   ‚Äì odoo:read_partners, odoo:write_sales, odoo:write_invoices, odoo:read_stock   ‚Äì woo:read_orders, woo:read_products   ‚Äì drive:read_docs, drive:write_docs   ‚Äì monday:write_items ‚Ä¢ Rate Limits (defaults): 60 rpm per tool, burst 120; adjustable by policy. ‚Ä¢ Response Envelope: { correlation_id, request_id, status, data|error }.3) MCP Tool Catalog ‚Äì Detailed Specs (v1)‚Ä¢ odoo.get_partnerRequest: { "email"?: string, "id"?: int }Rules: one of (email,id) requiredResponse: { id, name, email, vat, phone, company_type, street, city, zip, country, tags[] }Errors: not_found, permission_denied, invalid_requestScopes: odoo:read_partnersIdempotency: n/a (read)‚Ä¢ odoo.create_quotationRequest: { "partner_id": int, "currency": "EUR", "lines": [ { "sku"?: string, "product_id"?: int, "qty": float, "price"?: float, "discount"?: float, "tax_code"?: string } ], "external_id"?: string }Resolution: if sku present ‚Üí map to product_id; else product_id must be provided.Response: { order_id, number, state: "draft", external_id }Errors: product_not_found, partner_not_found, validation_errorScopes: odoo:write_salesIdempotency: external_id REQUIRED‚Ä¢ odoo.post_invoiceRequest: { "order_id": int, "post": true, "external_id": string }Response: { invoice_id, number, state: "posted", pdf_url?: string }Preconditions: order must be confirmed/paid per policyScopes: odoo:write_invoicesIdempotency: external_id REQUIRED‚Ä¢ odoo.stock_availabilityRequest: { "product_id"?: int, "sku"?: string }Response: { product_id, sku, on_hand: float, reserved: float, available: float, locations: [ { "name": str, "qty": float } ] }Scopes: odoo:read_stockIdempotency: n/a‚Ä¢ woo.get_orderRequest: { "order_id": int }Response: { id, number, status, payment_status, total, currency, email, phone, lines: [ { sku, name, qty, price, vat_rate } ], created_at }Scopes: woo:read_orders‚Ä¢ woo.list_ordersRequest: { "status"?: string, "created_after"?: iso8601, "limit"?: int=50 }Response: { items: [ ... ], next_cursor?: string }Scopes: woo:read_orders‚Ä¢ drive.search_docsRequest: { "query": string, "folder"?: string, "mime_types"?: [string] }Response: { results: [ { id, name, path, mime_type, modified_at } ] }Scopes: drive:read_docs‚Ä¢ drive.append_noteRequest: { "doc_id": string, "text": string, "meta"?: { "source": string, "author": string } }Response: { doc_id, appended_at }Scopes: drive:write_docs‚Ä¢ monday.create_itemRequest: { "board": string, "group"?: string, "columns": { "name": string, ... } }Response: { item_id, board, url }Scopes: monday:write_items‚Ä¢ crm.create_ticketRequest: { "contact": { "email": string, "name"?: string }, "subject": string, "body": string, "priority"?: string }Response: { ticket_id, url }Scopes: odoo:write_crm (or helpdesk)4) End-to-End Sequences (E2E)A) Dealer Registration (B2B)1. Trigger: Woo signup (role=Dealer) ‚Üí webhook ‚Üí n8n (DLQ-safe).2. n8n: validate payload, deduplicate by email; upsert partner via MCP: odoo.get_partner ‚Üí odoo.create_quotation(optional welcome pack) with external_id=‚Äúdealer:{email}:{timestamp}‚Äù.3. Points setup (myCred via n8n or direct API). 4. Monday: monday.create_item(board='Dealer Onboarding', columns{ status='New', email, company }).5. Drive: drive.append_note with the onboarding log.6. AI: Hairo Assistant can answer ‚Äúdealer status‚Äù by calling odoo.get_partner + Monday board read (read-only via MCP proxy).B) Order-to-Cash (B2C/B2B)1. Trigger: Woo order.paid.2. n8n: woo.get_order ‚Üí partner match in Odoo ‚Üí odoo.create_quotation (or SO) using external_id=‚Äúwoo:{order_id}‚Äù ‚Üí confirm ‚Üí odoo.post_invoice.3. Stock allocation: odoo.stock_availability to verify; if insufficient, set Monday alert.4. Invoice PDF archived to Drive; customer email via Zapier (if needed).5. Status roundtrip to Woo (shipment &amp; tracking).C) Returns (RMA)1. Trigger: customer return request (site form).2. n8n: create Odoo RMA/return; credit note after inspection.3. Drive: append return record; Monday: update incident board.4. AI: explains return status using policy docs + Odoo data.D) Loyalty &amp; Affiliates1. Trigger: order delivered / affiliate conversion.2. n8n: compute points, update Odoo &amp; myCred; create Drive ledger entry.3. AI: responds to ‚Äúpoints balance‚Äù by reading Odoo/myCred via MCP.5) Validation Rules &amp; Idempotency‚Ä¢ external_id is mandatory for create/confirm/post operations (odoo.*). ‚Ä¢ Duplicate detection: same external_id ‚Üí safe no-op. ‚Ä¢ Numeric validations: qty &gt; 0; price ‚â• 0; VAT code exists in Odoo. ‚Ä¢ Partner resolution order: id ‚Üí email ‚Üí phone. ‚Ä¢ Stock checks occur before invoice posting when policy requires reservation. ‚Ä¢ Monetary rounding: 2 decimals, EUR; VAT per Odoo tax tables.6) Error Model &amp; Retries‚Ä¢ Error Types: invalid_request, permission_denied, not_found, conflict, rate_limited, upstream_error, timeout. ‚Ä¢ Retry Policy: 3 retries (250ms, 1s, 5s); do not retry invalid_request/permission_denied. ‚Ä¢ Dead-Letter Queue: after retries, push to n8n DLQ; create Monday item ‚ÄúIntegration Incident‚Äù. ‚Ä¢ Correlation: include correlation_id in all logs; propagate to Monday.7) Security Controls‚Ä¢ Secrets vault with quarterly rotation; per-service accounts in Odoo/Woo. ‚Ä¢ Field-level privacy: mask PII in logs; redact tokens in traces. ‚Ä¢ Access scopes per tool; deny by default; allow only explicit actions. ‚Ä¢ HITL gates for high-risk actions (refunds, credit notes, mass price changes).8) Testing Strategy (UAT &amp; Staging)‚Ä¢ Environments: STAGING (mirror of Odoo, Woo sandboxes) and PRODUCTION. ‚Ä¢ Unit tests for MCP tool schemas (happy path + validation failures). ‚Ä¢ Flow tests in n8n: mock webhooks; verify idempotency and retries. ‚Ä¢ Shadow mode: run MCP tools in read-only with production traffic for a week before enabling writes. ‚Ä¢ UAT scripts stored in Drive: /QA/UAT_AI_Integration_Checklists/.9) Monitoring &amp; KPIs‚Ä¢ MCP latency p95 &lt; 800ms; success rate ‚â• 99%. ‚Ä¢ Order sync time &lt; 60s; stock sync &lt; 5m; invoice posting &lt; 2m. ‚Ä¢ Incident MTTR &lt; 2h; failed jobs per day &lt; 3. ‚Ä¢ Dashboards: Monday boards ‚ÄúOps ‚Äì Integrations‚Äù, ‚ÄúSales ‚Äì Pipeline‚Äù, ‚ÄúFinance ‚Äì Invoicing‚Äù.10) Rollout Checklist1. Provision MCP endpoint with TLS; set scopes. 2. Create Odoo service users and API keys (read/write separated). 3. Configure Woo REST keys (read-only for catalog, write for orders). 4. Deploy n8n on OVH; import baseline flows; enable logs and DLQ. 5. Configure Zapier zaps for marketing &amp; communications. 6. Create Monday boards and columns for incidents/KPIs. 7. Set Drive folder structure and permissions; enable versioning. 8. Run staging tests; validate UAT; enable shadow mode; go-live. 9. Schedule backups; document DR plan; run tabletop exercise. 10. Establish on-call and escalation policy.11) Appendix ‚Äì Sample PayloadsA) odoo.create_quotationRequest:{  "partner_id": 1234,  "currency": "EUR",  "external_id": "woo:987654",  "lines": [    { "sku": "BEARD-OIL-50", "qty": 2, "price": 14.90, "tax_code": "DE-STD-19" },    { "sku": "BEARD-BALM-50", "qty": 1, "price": 12.90, "tax_code": "DE-STD-19" }  ]}Response:{ "order_id": 5566, "number": "SO0005566", "state": "draft", "external_id": "woo:987654" }B) drive.append_noteRequest:{  "doc_id": "1A2B3C",  "text": "Dealer onboarding completed for email test@example.com",  "meta": { "source": "n8n", "author": "system" }}Response:{ "doc_id": "1A2B3C", "appended_at": "2025-10-12T09:40:00Z" }

Phase 8 ‚Äì Data Knowledge Graph &amp; AI MemoryBuilding the Cognitive Core of the HAIROTICMEN Intelligent System1 ¬∑ ObjectiveTo design and implement a unified corporate knowledge infrastructure that connects all data sources (Drive, Odoo, WooCommerce, CRM, Finance, Marketing, Programs) into a continuously updated Knowledge Graph and AI Memory.This allows Hairo Assistant to answer, predict, and decide using full company context.2 ¬∑ Core Concept[Raw Data] ‚Üí [Structured Knowledge] ‚Üí [Graph Links] ‚Üí [AI Embeddings] ‚Üí [Continuous Learning]Every file, record, and metric becomes a knowledge node, semantically linked to others (product ‚Üí program ‚Üí partner ‚Üí finance ‚Üí policy).3 ¬∑ Knowledge Graph Architecture                     ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê                     ‚îÇ   HAIRO_AI Core Memory‚îÇ                     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¨‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò                                  ‚îÇ        ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¨‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îº‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¨‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê        ‚îÇ              ‚îÇ          ‚îÇ              ‚îÇ             ‚îÇ [Products]     [Programs]   [Operations]   [Finance]   [Governance]        ‚îÇ              ‚îÇ          ‚îÇ              ‚îÇ             ‚îÇ  (Odoo + Woo)   (Loyalty,Stand) (SOPs,Logs) (Invoices,BWA) (GDPR,Audit)Node Types: Product ¬∑ Partner ¬∑ Customer ¬∑ Document ¬∑ Policy ¬∑ TransactionRelations: uses / belongs to / affects / regulated by / updated byStored as a graph database (e.g., Neo4j Community or LiteGraph via JSON) and mirrored in MCP Memory for vector search.4 ¬∑ Data Sources &amp; PipelinesSourceTypeConnectorDestination NodeGoogle DriveDocs / PDF / ImagesDrive API + MCP IndexerKnowledge Graph &gt; DocumentsOdoo ERP 17Sales / Finance / InventoryOdoo API (v17 REST)Nodes: Order, Invoice, StockWooCommerceOrders / CustomersWoo REST APINodes: Customer, OrdermyCred &amp; SliceWPLoyalty / Partner Datan8n workflowNodes: Program, PartnerMonday.comKPIs / TasksMonday APINode: Performance MetricZapier FeedsAds / LeadsZapier webhooksNode: Marketing EventData flows daily via n8n to the central Graph Builder process.5 ¬∑ Knowledge Schema (Example Model)Node TypeKey FieldsRelationshipsProductname, SKU, CNPN, category, ingredientslinked_to ‚Üí Marketing Campaign, InvoicePartnerID, location, tierassociated_with ‚Üí Stand ProgramCustomerID, loyalty points, tierpurchases ‚Üí ProductInvoiceID, amount, VAT %, dateissued_by ‚Üí OdooPolicytitle, version, compliance tagregulates ‚Üí ProcessProcess / SOPstep_list, departmentsupports ‚Üí Agent6 ¬∑ MCP AI Memory StructureMemory LayerPurposeStorage MethodShort-TermActive context (current conversation, workflow)Redis cache / MCP sessionMid-TermRecent 30-day eventsSQL lite storeLong-TermFull Knowledge Graph (vectorized)Vector DB (e.g., FAISS / Pinecone)Data Volume: up to 20 GB textual + 50 GB file metadata ‚Üí indexed nightly.Access: secure tokens per Agent; Governance AI monitors reads/writes.7 ¬∑ Knowledge Ingestion Pipeline1Ô∏è‚É£  Extract ‚Üí via APIs / File Crawlers2Ô∏è‚É£  Transform ‚Üí clean + tag (department, date, owner)3Ô∏è‚É£  Load ‚Üí into Graph DB + Vector Memory4Ô∏è‚É£  Validate ‚Üí Governance AI checks accuracy5Ô∏è‚É£  Embed ‚Üí Hairo Assistant updates contextual modelFrequency = Daily (full sync at 03:00 CEST).8 ¬∑ Metadata Tagging StandardsTag PrefixMeaningExamplePROD_Product infoPROD_BEARDKIT_6IN1PROG_Program filePROG_LOYALTY_TIER1FIN_Finance docFIN_VAT_Q3_2025GOV_ComplianceGOV_GDPR_POLICY_V4SOP_Standard ProcedureSOP_SALES_REFUNDMKT_Marketing AssetMKT_TIKTOK_CAMP45Each file‚Äôs metadata appended as YAML header during indexing.9 ¬∑ AI Query and Retrieval LogicWhen any AI Agent requests info:User/Agent Query     ‚ÜìSemantic Search ‚Üí Vector Index     ‚ÜìKnowledge Graph Traversal ‚Üí related nodes     ‚ÜìGovernance AI filters permissions     ‚ÜìHairo Assistant composes answer / actionExample:‚ÄúShow me last month‚Äôs dealer commissions in Berlin.‚Äù‚Üí Partner AI + Finance AI pulls linked nodes (Partner: Berlin ‚Üí Invoices ‚Üí Finance Reports).10 ¬∑ Security &amp; GovernanceAccess Control: token-based by role (Agent / Human / Board).Encryption: AES-256 at-rest / TLS 1.3 in-transit.Data Provenance: every node includes source URL + checksum.Governance AI Logs: every query ‚Üí timestamped audit record.Retention: 3 months raw logs, 12 months aggregated, 10 years financial.11 ¬∑ Governance AI ResponsibilitiesFunctionDescriptionValidationchecks for missing links / duplicatesBias Controlensures neutral decision suggestionsData Lifecyclemanages archival and deletionCompliance Reportsgenerates monthly GDPR summaryDrift Monitoringdetects knowledge staleness &gt; 90 days12 ¬∑ Practical Example: Knowledge Graph in ActionScenario: A customer buys a Beard OilWooCommerce Order ‚Üí Odoo Invoice ‚Üí Loyalty Reward ‚Üí Stock Update ‚Üí Campaign TrackingKnowledge Graph links automatically:Product ‚Üí Customer ‚Üí Invoice ‚Üí Program ‚Üí Marketing Campaign ‚Üí Finance RecordNow, Hairo Assistant can answer:‚ÄúHow many Beard Oil sales came from TikTok campaigns in Germany last month, and what was the average loyalty points issued?‚ÄùInstant cross-system answer with audit trace.13 ¬∑ Memory Maintenance ScheduleFrequencyTaskOwnerDailyIncremental sync (Drive + Odoo)Governance AIWeeklyRelationship integrity checkHairo AssistantMonthlyStale data purge &gt; 2 %Knowledge coverage &lt; 95 %Outdated content &gt; 90 days.15 ¬∑ Expected OutcomesA living, self-updating knowledge ecosystem.All HAIROTICMEN agents share one semantic memory.90 % reduction in information retrieval time.Decisions become context-aware and consistent.Seamless integration with future brands under MH Trading UG.16 ¬∑ Next Phase TransitionNext we move to Phase 9 ‚Äì Live Testing &amp; Validation (UAT Phase 2),where we‚Äôll test the Knowledge Graph and AI Memory in live conditions ‚Äî verifying data retrieval accuracy, response speed, and compliance logging.Footer¬© 2025 MH Trading UG ‚Äì All Rights Reserved | Polierweg 39, 12351 Berlin | info@hairoticmen.de |

Risk ID	Description	Likelihood	Impact	Rating	Owner	Mitigations	Linked Controls	Status	Notes
R-001	PII leakage via prompts or outputs	Medium	High	High	DPO	Guardrails, redaction, human review for sensitive replies	C-AI-002, C-AI-008, C-AI-001	Open	Block raw PII in logs; AI=MetadataOnly for sensitive datasets
R-002	Unauthorized tool or agent used in production	Low	High	Medium	ITSec	RBAC, Zap/OAuth scope reviews, change management	C-AI-006, C-AI-010, C-AI-013	Open	Approve via Review_Log before enabling
R-003	Model quality regression after config change	Medium	Medium	Medium	AI Lead	Eval regression suite, canary tests, rollback	C-AI-005, C-AI-010	Open	Block deploy if evals fail critical tests
R-004	Broken connector / integration outage	Medium	Medium	Medium	IT	Retries, signatures, monitoring alerts	C-AI-004, C-AI-014	Open	Fail safely; queue requests for replay
R-005	Secret leakage inside sheets or repos	Low	High	Medium	Security Lead	Secrets Vault, monthly rotation, scans	C-AI-003, C-AI-010	Open	No secrets in sheets; store names only
R-006	Over-permissive Zap or OAuth scopes	Low	Medium	Low	AI Ops	Scopes review; webhook read/send only	C-AI-006	Open	Reduce scopes; service accounts read-only
R-007	Retention non‚Äëcompliance (data kept too long)	Low	High	Medium	Security/DPO	Automated purge per RETENTION; audit trail	C-AI-009, C-AI-014	Open	Spot checks quarterly
R-008	Prompt injection / data exfiltration via RAG	Medium	High	High	Security Lead	Whitelist sources; content sanitization; deny tools by default	C-AI-001, C-AI-002	Open	No external URLs ingestion without review
R-009	Affiliate payout mismatch / fraud	Low	High	Medium	Finance Lead	Reconciliation checks; dual-control approvals	C-AI-014, C-AI-012	Open	SliceWP is read-only for AI
R-010	Availability SLO breach for assistants	Low	Medium	Low	IT/Ops	HA, alerting, error budgets	C-AI-004	Open	Escalation P1 if <99.5% daily
R-011	Backup not restorable or corrupted	Low	High	Medium	IT	Restore drills, checksum verification	C-AI-014	Open	Quarterly full restore test
R-012	Unlicensed/expired brand asset used	Low	Medium	Low	Marketing Lead	Brand assets review & approvals	C-AI-010	Open	Public folder only; licensing verified

HAIROTICMEN ‚Äì Legal TemplatesA) Non-Disclosure Agreement (NDA)Mutual confidentiality, valid 3 years, governed by German law (Berlin). Includes IP protection and non-solicitation clause.B) Data Processing Agreement (DPA)Compliant with GDPR Art. 28. Defines Data Controller/Processor obligations, subprocessors, security, retention, and audit rights.C) Supplier ContractIncludes ISO 9001 / GMP compliance, delivery terms (CIF Berlin), warranty, liability caps, termination, and governing law.D) Compliance Audit FormQuarterly form to verify document validity, supplier registrations, LUCID/VerpackG filings, and CNPN conformity.
